旧说堂上之乐,jiu'shuo'tang'shang'zhi'le

就死意甚烈,jiu'si'yi'shen'lie
旧俗接鱼蚕,jiu'su'jie'yu'can

酒醒却忆儿童事,jiu'xing'que'yi'er'tong'shi
酒醒人散山寂寂,jiu'xing'ren'san'shan'ji'ji
